    SELECT COALESCE(sum(p1."Quantity"::numeric * e."TicketPrice"), 0.0)
    FROM (
        SELECT p2."EventId", p2."Quantity", date_part('month', p2."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"

    INNER JOIN "Events" AS e ON p1."EventId" = e."EventId"

    SELECT COALESCE(sum(p1."Quantity"::numeric * e."TicketPrice"), 0.0)

SELECT p0."Key", (
    SELECT COALESCE(sum(p1."Quantity"::numeric * e."TicketPrice"), 0.0)
    FROM (
        SELECT p2."EventId", p2."Quantity", date_part('month', p2."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"
        FROM "PurchasedEvents" AS p2
    ) AS p1
    INNER JOIN "Events" AS e ON p1."EventId" = e."EventId"
    WHERE p0."Key" = p1."Key" OR (p0."Key" IS NULL AND p1."Key" IS NULL))
FROM (
    SELECT date_part('month', p."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"
    FROM "PurchasedEvents" AS p
) AS p0

    SELECT COALESCE(sum(p1."Quantity"::numeric * e."TicketPrice"), 0.0)
    FROM (
        SELECT p2."EventId", p2."Quantity", date_part('month', p2."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"
        FROM "PurchasedEvents" AS p2
    ) AS p1
    INNER JOIN "Events" AS e ON p1."EventId" = e."EventId"
    WHERE p0."Key" = p1."Key" OR (p0."Key" IS NULL AND p1."Key" IS NULL))
FROM (
    SELECT date_part('month', p."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"
    FROM "PurchasedEvents" AS p
) AS p0
GROUP BY p0."Key"

    FROM "PurchasedEvents" AS p0

    SELECT COALESCE(sum(p1."Quantity"::numeric * e."TicketPrice"), 0.0)
    FROM (
        SELECT p2."EventId", p2."Quantity", date_part('month', p2."PurchaseDate" AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')::int AS "Key"
